## 7. ENGINE SKILLS NEEDED

### 7.1 Speed/Feed Calculator Engine Requirements

Based on audit, the calculator needs:

```yaml
PREREQUISITE_DATA:
  materials:
    required_fields:
      - kienzle.kc1_1     # Missing: 81.6%
      - kienzle.mc        # Missing: 81.6%
      - hardness.hrc      # Missing: 34%
      - thermal.conductivity  # Missing: 45%
    minimum_coverage: 70%
    current_coverage: 18.4%
    
  tools:
    required_fields:
      - geometry.cutting_edge_angle
      - geometry.rake_angle
      - coating.type
      - recommendations.materials
    minimum_coverage: 80%
    current_coverage: 45.9%
    
  machines:
    required_fields:
      - spindle.max_rpm
      - spindle.max_power
      - axis.max_feedrate
      - limits.rapid_feedrate
    minimum_coverage: 100%
    current_coverage: 60% (6 machines)

ENGINE_SKILLS_REQUIRED:
  1. prism-kienzle-force-model:
     purpose: Calculate cutting forces from kc1_1, mc
     inputs: [ap, ae, fz, material_kc]
     outputs: [Fc, Ff, Fp, power]
     
  2. prism-taylor-tool-life:
     purpose: Predict tool life from cutting parameters
     inputs: [Vc, material_C, material_n]
     outputs: [tool_life_minutes, cost_per_part]
     
  3. prism-thermal-model:
     purpose: Temperature prediction in cutting zone
     inputs: [Vc, fz, ap, material_thermal]
     outputs: [T_chip, T_workpiece, T_tool]
     
  4. prism-stability-lobe:
     purpose: Chatter prediction and avoidance
     inputs: [spindle_rpm, ap, tool_stiffness, holder_stiffness]
     outputs: [stable_ap_max, stability_ratio]
     
  5. prism-mrr-optimizer:
     purpose: Maximize MRR within all constraints
     inputs: [all_constraints, all_parameters]
     outputs: [optimal_Vc, optimal_fz, optimal_ap, optimal_ae, MRR]
     
  6. prism-uncertainty-engine:
     purpose: Propagate uncertainties through calculations
     inputs: [parameter_values, parameter_uncertainties]
     outputs: [result ¬± uncertainty (confidence)]
```

### 7.2 Post Processor Engine Requirements

```yaml
POST_PROCESSOR_ENGINE:
  analysis_skills:
    1. prism-gcode-parser:
       purpose: Parse and tokenize G-code files
       inputs: [nc_file_path]
       outputs: [parsed_blocks, motion_commands, parameters]

       purpose: Extract and analyze F commands
       inputs: [parsed_gcode]
       outputs: [feed_distribution, anomalies, optimization_opportunities]
       
    3. prism-speed-analyzer:
       purpose: Extract and analyze S commands
       inputs: [parsed_gcode]
       outputs: [speed_distribution, thermal_risk_zones]

       purpose: Predict machining time from G-code
       inputs: [parsed_gcode, machine_specs]
       outputs: [cycle_time, breakdown_by_operation]
       
    5. prism-optimization-suggester:
       purpose: Generate optimization recommendations
       inputs: [analysis_results, constraints]
       outputs: [suggestions_ranked_by_impact]

  modification_skills:
    6. prism-gcode-modifier:
       purpose: Apply approved changes to G-code
       inputs: [original_gcode, modifications]
       outputs: [modified_gcode, change_log]
```

```yaml
skill_id: prism-speed-feed-engine
version: 1.0.0
priority: P0-CRITICAL
status: NOT_CREATED

description: |
  Master skill for calculating optimal cutting parameters
  using physics-based models with empirical corrections.

prerequisites:
  - prism-material-physics (EXISTS)
  - prism-tool-schema (EXISTS)
  - prism-machine-schema (EXISTS)
  - prism-uncertainty-propagation (EXISTS)
  - prism-formula-evolution (EXISTS)
  - prism-dimensional-analysis (NOT CREATED)

inputs:
  - material_id: string (from materials database)
  - tool_id: string (from tools database - EMPTY!)
  - machine_id: string (from machines database - EMPTY!)
  - operation_type: enum [roughing, finishing, slotting, ...]
  - constraints: object (depth, width, power, etc.)

outputs:
  - cutting_speed: {value, uncertainty, unit, confidence}
  - feed_per_tooth: {value, uncertainty, unit, confidence}
  - axial_depth: {value, uncertainty, unit, confidence}
  - radial_depth: {value, uncertainty, unit, confidence}
  - mrr: {value, uncertainty, unit, confidence}
  - power_required: {value, uncertainty, unit, confidence}
  - force_components: {Fx, Fy, Fz with uncertainties}
  - tool_deflection: {value, uncertainty, unit, confidence}
  - surface_finish: {Ra, uncertainty, unit, confidence}
  - recommendations: array of optimization suggestions

master_equations:
  - F-SPEED-001: Vc = (œÄ √ó D √ó N) / 1000
  - F-FEED-001: vf = fz √ó z √ó N
  - F-POWER-001: P = (Fc √ó Vc) / (60000 √ó Œ∑)
  - F-FORCE-001: Fc = kc1_1 √ó ap √ó fz^(1-mc) √ó KŒ≥ √ó Kv √ó Kmat
  - F-DEFLECT-001: Œ¥ = (F √ó L¬≥) / (3 √ó E √ó I)
  - F-MRR-001: MRR = ap √ó ae √ó vf

validation_requirements:
  - Physics validation (conservation laws)
  - Dimensional analysis (unit consistency)
  - Bounds checking (physical limits)
  - Cross-reference (empirical data)
  - Historical validation (past results)

dependencies_blocking:
  - Tools database: 0 cutting tools
  - Machines database: 0 records
  - Material completion: 17.8% on critical params
```

## 7. ENGINE SKILLS REQUIREMENTS

### Speed/Feed Calculator Engine Skill Specification

```yaml
skill_id: prism-speed-feed-calculator-engine
version: 1.0.0
priority: P0 - CRITICAL
status: NOT CREATED

purpose: |
  Core computational engine that consumes material, tool, and machine data
  to produce optimized speed/feed recommendations with uncertainty quantification.

dependencies:
  required_databases:
    - materials_db: "3,518 materials with machining parameters"
    - tools_db: "Cutting tools with geometry and limits"
    - machines_db: "Machine capabilities and limits"
    - matrices_db: "Material-tool compatibility matrices"
  
  required_skills:
    - prism-formula-harmony: "Master equation management"
    - prism-dimensional-analysis: "Unit verification"
    - prism-uncertainty-propagation: "Error propagation"
    - prism-calculation-validator: "Output validation"
    - prism-machine-integration: "Machine limit checks"

master_equations:
  F-SPEED-001:
    formula: "V_c = (œÄ √ó D √ó n) / 1000"
    inputs: [diameter_mm, rpm]
    output: cutting_speed_m_min
    uncertainty_sources: [diameter_tolerance, rpm_accuracy]
  
  F-FEED-001:
    formula: "f = f_z √ó z √ó n"
    inputs: [feed_per_tooth_mm, flute_count, rpm]
    output: feed_rate_mm_min
    uncertainty_sources: [feed_tolerance, flute_count_accuracy]
  
  F-POWER-001:
    formula: "P_c = (k_c1.1 √ó b √ó h^(1-m_c) √ó V_c) / (60 √ó 10^6 √ó Œ∑)"
    inputs: [specific_cutting_force, width_of_cut, chip_thickness, cutting_speed, efficiency]
    output: cutting_power_kW
    uncertainty_sources: [kc1_1_uncertainty, geometry_tolerance, efficiency_range]
  
  F-MRR-001:
    formula: "MRR = a_p √ó a_e √ó f"
    inputs: [depth_of_cut_mm, width_of_cut_mm, feed_rate_mm_min]
    output: material_removal_rate_cm3_min
    uncertainty_sources: [all_input_tolerances]

computational_pipeline:
  1_input_validation:
    - Verify all required parameters present
    - Check dimensional consistency
    - Validate ranges against physics limits
  
  2_data_retrieval:
    - Fetch material properties (kc1_1, mc, hardness, thermal)
    - Fetch tool geometry (diameter, flutes, helix, max_rpm)
    - Fetch machine limits (power, torque, rpm_range)
  
  3_base_calculation:
    - Compute starting point from recommendations
    - Apply material adjustment factors
    - Apply tool adjustment factors
  
  4_constraint_application:
    - Check power limits
    - Check torque limits  
    - Check deflection limits
    - Check thermal limits
    - Check stability (chatter)
  
  5_optimization:
    - Maximize MRR within all constraints
    - Apply safety margins
    - Compute uncertainty bounds
  
  6_output_generation:
    - Primary recommendation with uncertainty
    - Alternative strategies
    - Limiting factors explanation
    - XAI reasoning

output_format:
  recommendation:
    rpm: {value: int, uncertainty: float, ci: 0.95}
    feed_rate: {value: float, unit: "mm/min", uncertainty: float}
    depth_of_cut: {value: float, unit: "mm", uncertainty: float}
    width_of_cut: {value: float, unit: "mm", uncertainty: float}
    mrr: {value: float, unit: "cm¬≥/min", uncertainty: float}
    power_required: {value: float, unit: "kW", uncertainty: float}
  
  constraints:
    limiting_factor: string
    margin_to_limits: dict
    safety_factor_applied: float
  
  explanation:
    reasoning: string
    data_sources: list
    confidence_level: float
    alternative_strategies: list
```

```yaml
  calculate_rpm:
    inputs: [V_c, diameter]
    outputs: [N ¬± uncertainty, unit: rev/min]
    formula: N = (V_c √ó 1000) / (œÄ √ó D)
    
  calculate_feed_rate:
    inputs: [f_z, z, N]
    outputs: [f_m ¬± uncertainty, unit: mm/min]
    formula: f_m = f_z √ó z √ó N
    
  calculate_mrr:
    inputs: [DOC, WOC, f_m]
    outputs: [MRR ¬± uncertainty, unit: cm¬≥/min]
    formula: MRR = DOC √ó WOC √ó f_m / 1000
    
  calculate_power:
    inputs: [k_c, b, h, V_c, efficiency]
    outputs: [P_c ¬± uncertainty, unit: kW]
    formula: F-POWER-001
    
  calculate_force:
    inputs: [k_c1_1, m_c, b, h]
    outputs: [F_c ¬± uncertainty, unit: N]
    formula: F-FORCE-001 (Kienzle)
    
  optimize_mrr:
    inputs: [constraints, targets]
    outputs: [optimal_parameters, MRR_max, limiting_factor]
    method: constrained_optimization

constraint_handlers:
  machine_limits: [spindle_rpm_max, power_max, torque_max]
  tool_limits: [deflection_max, temperature_max, wear_rate]
  process_limits: [chatter_frequency, surface_finish_min]

uncertainty_model:
  method: monte_carlo
  samples: 1000
  confidence_level: 0.95
  propagation: automatic

wiring:
  consumes: [materials_db, tools_db, machines_db, tool_holders_db]
  produces: [cutting_parameters, forces, power, mrr]
  hooks: [preCalculate, postCalculate, constraintViolation, optimizationComplete]

effort_estimate:

  unit: tool_calls
  confidence: 0.80
```

#### 7.1 Speed/Feed Calculator Engine Skill Requirements

```yaml
skill_name: prism-speed-feed-engine
version: 1.0.0
priority: P0-CRITICAL
status: SPECIFICATION

requirements:
  inputs:
    - material_id: string (links to materials_db)
    - tool_id: string (links to tools_db)
    - machine_id: string (links to machines_db)
    - operation_type: enum [ROUGHING, FINISHING, SEMI-FINISHING]
    - geometry:
        depth_of_cut: float (mm) ¬± uncertainty
        width_of_cut: float (mm) ¬± uncertainty
        workpiece_dimensions: array[3]
    - constraints:
        max_power: float (kW)
        max_torque: float (Nm)
        max_deflection: float (mm)
        surface_finish_target: float (Ra, ¬µm)
    
  outputs:
    - spindle_speed: 
        value: float (RPM)
        uncertainty: float
        confidence: float (0-1)
    - feed_rate:
        value: float (mm/min)
        uncertainty: float
        confidence: float (0-1)
    - feed_per_tooth:
        value: float (mm/tooth)
        uncertainty: float
        confidence: float (0-1)
    - mrr:
        value: float (cm¬≥/min)
        uncertainty: float
        confidence: float (0-1)
    - cutting_force:
        components: [Fx, Fy, Fz]
        resultant: float (N)
        uncertainty: float
    - power_required:
        value: float (kW)
        uncertainty: float
    - limiting_factor: enum [POWER, TORQUE, DEFLECTION, SURFACE_FINISH, TOOL_LIMIT, MACHINE_LIMIT]
    - confidence_level: enum [HIGH, MEDIUM, LOW, UNCERTAIN]
    - recommendations: array[string]
    
  dependencies:
    required:
      - materials_db: complete kienzle, johnson_cook, taylor data
      - tools_db: complete geometry, grades, limits
      - machines_db: complete power, speed, torque curves
      - matrices_db: material-tool-operation compatibility
    optional:
      - historical_results: for ML calibration
      - real_time_sensors: for adaptive adjustment
      
  master_equations:
    - F-SPEED-001: V = œÄ √ó D √ó n / 1000 ‚Üí n = V √ó 1000 / (œÄ √ó D)
    - F-FEED-001: vf = fz √ó z √ó n
    - F-POWER-001: P = Fc √ó Vc / (60 √ó 1000 √ó Œ∑)
    - F-FORCE-001: Fc = kc1_1 √ó b √ó h^(1-mc)
    - F-DEFLECT-001: Œ¥ = F √ó L¬≥ / (3 √ó E √ó I)
    - F-MRR-001: MRR = ae √ó ap √ó vf / 1000
    
  verification:
    - physics_check: forces, power, thermal within bounds
    - empirical_check: compare to machining_advisor data
    - historical_check: compare to past cuts
    - uncertainty_propagation: through entire calculation chain
    
  hooks:
    pre_calculate: [validate_inputs, check_compatibility, verify_completeness]
    post_calculate: [verify_physics, check_limits, propagate_uncertainty]
    on_error: [graceful_degrade, use_fallbacks, log_failure]
```

```yaml
SKILL: prism-speed-feed-engine
VERSION: 1.0.0
STATUS: SPECIFICATION_ONLY
PRIORITY: P0

REQUIRED_CAPABILITIES:
  core_calculations:
    - spindle_speed_from_sfm:
        formula: "N = (SFM √ó 12) / (œÄ √ó D)"
        inputs: [surface_feet_per_minute, diameter_inches]
        output: rpm ¬± uncertainty
        validation: physics_validator, dimensional_verifier
    
    - feed_rate_from_chip_load:
        formula: "F = f_z √ó z √ó N"
        inputs: [chip_load_per_tooth, teeth_count, rpm]
        output: ipm ¬± uncertainty
        validation: physics_validator, tool_deflection_checker
    
    - material_removal_rate:
        formula: "MRR = WOC √ó DOC √ó F"
        inputs: [width_of_cut, depth_of_cut, feed_rate]
        output: cubic_inches_per_minute ¬± uncertainty
        validation: power_checker, thermal_checker
    
    - cutting_power:
        formula: "P = (MRR √ó k_s) / Œ∑"
        inputs: [mrr, specific_cutting_force, efficiency]
        output: horsepower ¬± uncertainty
        validation: spindle_power_limit_checker
    
    - tool_deflection:
        formula: "Œ¥ = (F √ó L¬≥) / (3 √ó E √ó I)"
        inputs: [cutting_force, stick_out, modulus, moment_of_inertia]
        output: inches ¬± uncertainty

    - surface_finish_estimate:
        formula: "Ra = f¬≤ / (32 √ó r)"
        inputs: [feed_per_rev, corner_radius]
        output: microinches ¬± uncertainty
        validation: geometry_validator

  constraint_handling:
    - spindle_speed_limits: "N_min ‚â§ N ‚â§ N_max"
```

### 7.1 Speed/Feed Calculator Engine Skill

```yaml
skill_id: prism-speed-feed-engine
version: "1.0.0"
priority: P0
tier: CRITICAL

dependencies:
  required:
    - materials_database (‚â•80% complete)
    - cutting_tools_database (‚â•50 tools)
    - machine_database (‚â•5 machines)
    - material_tool_matrix (populated)
  optional:
    - tool_holder_database
    - coolant_database

inputs:
  required:
    - material_id: string
    - tool_id: string
    - operation: enum[FACE, POCKET, SLOT, DRILL, BORE, THREAD]
    - depth_of_cut: number (mm) ¬± uncertainty
    - width_of_cut: number (mm) ¬± uncertainty
  optional:
    - machine_id: string
    - surface_finish_target: number (¬µm)
    - mrr_target: number (cm¬≥/min)
    - tool_life_target: number (minutes)

outputs:
  primary:
    - spindle_speed: number (RPM) ¬± uncertainty
    - feed_rate: number (mm/min) ¬± uncertainty
    - feed_per_tooth: number (mm/tooth) ¬± uncertainty
    - mrr: number (cm¬≥/min) ¬± uncertainty
    - tool_life_estimate: number (minutes) ¬± uncertainty
    - power_required: number (kW) ¬± uncertainty
  secondary:
    - cutting_force: vector (N) ¬± uncertainty
    - temperature_estimate: number (¬∞C) ¬± uncertainty
    - surface_finish_predicted: number (¬µm) ¬± uncertainty
    - deflection_estimate: number (mm) ¬± uncertainty
  validation:
    - within_machine_limits: boolean
    - within_tool_limits: boolean
    - within_stability_limits: boolean
    - confidence_level: percentage

master_equations:
  - F-SPEED-001: v = œÄ √ó D √ó n / 1000
  - F-FEED-001: f = fz √ó z √ó n
  - F-POWER-001: P = (kc1.1 √ó h^(-mc) √ó ap √ó ae √ó vf) / (60 √ó 10^6 √ó Œ∑)
  - F-DEFLECT-001: Œ¥ = F √ó L¬≥ / (3 √ó E √ó I)
  - F-SURFACE-001: Ra = fz¬≤ / (32 √ó r) √ó 1000
  - F-MRR-001: MRR = ap √ó ae √ó vf

constraints:
  - n ‚â§ machine.max_spindle_speed
  - P ‚â§ machine.spindle_power √ó 0.8
  - Œ¥ ‚â§ tool.max_deflection
  - F_r ‚â§ tool.radial_force_limit
  - n ‚â• n_stability_min (chatter avoidance)

validation_rules:
  - dimensional_analysis: ALL inputs/outputs must have units
  - physics_bounds: ALL outputs must be physically reasonable
  - empirical_check: Results must fall within ¬±30% of handbook values
  - uncertainty_propagation: Output uncertainty must reflect input uncertainties
```
